He is wearing the same yellow suede jacket and jeans, holding a brown leather duffel bag tightly across his shoulder. The bike is suspended in mid-air against a backdrop of a massive waterfall. Cinematic lighting with sunbeams piercing through the forest canopy. High-fidelity textures on the denim and leather. 1:1 Aspect Ratio.

### 3. 英国版《Vogue》封面风格高端绅士肖像提示

**Author**: [John](https://x.com/john87445528)  **Date**: 2026-01-08  **Language**: zh

> 这是一个极其详细的多段式提示，旨在生成一张《英国版 Vogue》封面风格的高端时尚肖像。它要求严格遵循参考图像（参考图 1）的外观，同时采用另一张参考图像（参考图 2）的姿势、造型（细条纹西装、卷边袖口、折叠椅、单色调）以及轻松、精致的氛围。该提示包含核心指令、严格的生物特征再现规则、情感指导和详细的造型规范。

![英国版《Vogue》封面风格高端绅士肖像提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767967507476_hm05dx_G-JNXioWgAAyiHm.jpg)

```
究極統合プロンプト - 『British Vogue』ファッション誌表紙版
参照画像1のルックス × 参照画像2のハイエンド紳士美学

【核心指令】
世界的なファッションフォトグラファー（Steven Meisel/Paolo Roversi/Peter Lindbergh）として、**[参考画像1の人物]**のために『British Vogue』誌の表紙スタイルにふさわしいハイエンドなファッションポートレートを制作せよ。
四大核心要件：

1. 参考画像1の人物の外見的特徴（髪型、顔の輪郭、顔立ち、年齢感、体型など）を100%厳密に再現すること（一切の事前設定や仮定を行わない）
2. 気品ある優雅さの転換（参考図1人物の本来の気質→リラックスした高級感あるファッション紳士のオーラへ変換）
3. 参考図2のビジュアルDNAを完全に取り入れる（頬杖をついた座り姿勢、細ストライプのスーツ、折りたたみ椅子、純白背景、モノクロトーン、リラックスした洗練された雰囲気）
4. クリエイティブな微調整を許可 （中核的美学を維持した上で柔軟な調整可）

【一、人物容貌再現 - 参考図1】
✅ 絶対原則：参考図1を100%再現
完全保持必須の特徴：

髪型：髪の長さ、髪色、スタイル、カール度、生え際、ボリューム等 - 完全一致
顔型：輪郭、幅、顎ライン、顔の比率 - 完全保持
五官：目、鼻、唇、耳の形状・サイズ・位置・比率 - 完全一致
肌：肌色、質感、ほくろ、傷跡、シミ等 - 完全保持
年齢的特徴：しわ、小じわ、目の下のたるみ、ほうれい線等 - リアルに再現
体型：プロポーション、肩幅、全体的な体格 - 完全保持
固有の特徴：個人特有の顔面特徴または身体的特徴

❌ 絶対禁止事項：

参照画像1のいかなる外見的特徴も変更してはならない
参照画像1の特徴を「最適化」または「美化」してはならない
参照画像1がどうあるべきかを事前設定または仮定してはならない
参照画像2のスタイルを理由に参照画像1の外見を変更してはならない

✅ 検証基準：

参考図1の人物を知る視聴者が即座に同一人物と認識できること
顔の特徴類似度が95%以上であること
「参考図1に似ていない」との指摘があれば失敗

【二、表情と雰囲気 - 気品あるリラックスした紳士】
雰囲気転換の方向性：
核心となる感情キーワード：

「リラックスした自信」
「怠惰の中の洗練」
「さりげない高級感」
「芸術的な距離感」
「ファッショナブルな紳士の余裕」

顔の表情（参考図2のスタイル）：
眼差し：

✅ 軽く目線を上げ、カメラをまっすぐ見つめる

緩やかながらも鋭い眼差し
「私はリラックスしているが、自分の魅力を自覚している」と伝える
芸術的な距離感を帯びた観察眼
わざとらしくなく、力を入れず、媚びない

口元：

✅ 口角を軽く引き締めるか自然に閉じる

笑わず、真剣でもない
完全にリラックスした自然な状態
「さりげない洗練」を伝える
軽く唇をすぼめる選択も可能（抑制された優雅さ）

顔全体の印象：

✅ 顔の筋肉を完全にリラックスさせる

緊張や作為的な動きは一切なし
自然で、リラックスし、余裕のある状態
「証明する必要はない」というメッセージを伝える

✅ 肌の質感を自然に表現

適度な補正を施しつつリアルさを残す
ハイエンドで洗練された、しかし偽りのない質感

ディレクターによる感情誘導：

「あなたは『Vogue』の表紙を飾る人物。とてもリラックスしている」
「ポーズを取っているのではなく、ただここに座っているだけ」
「あなたの気だるさは本物で、演技ではない」
「ファッションは力むことではなく、リラックスすること」

【三、コアポーズ - 座った姿勢で頬杖（参考図2の定番ポーズ）】
象徴的なポーズ：
折りたたみ椅子に座る：

✅ 座り方：

簡易折りたたみ金属椅子に座る
体をやや前傾させるか自然に背筋を伸ばす
両脚は自然に開く（肩幅かやや広め）
両足は地面に平らに置く

手の姿勢（核心特徴）：

✅ 片手で頬を支える（図2標準参照）：

右手または左手の肘を同側の太ももに置く
掌または指で顎/頬を支える
一見無造作ながら洗練された印象
「思索」または「ゆったり待つ」状態を表現

✅ もう一方の手：

椅子の背もたれ/肘掛けに自然に置く
または自然に垂らす
あるいは反対側の太ももに軽く置く

姿勢の意義：

フォーマルな堅苦しさを打破
「リラックスした高級感」のファッション性を演出
「芸術/人生について考えている」というメッセージを伝える
日常道具（折りたたみ椅子）＋ 高級スタイリング ＝ 対比美学

身体姿勢：

肩の力を抜く（肩を上げない）
背骨を自然に曲げる（硬直しない）
全体として快適・自然・余裕を伝える

頭部の姿勢：

頭をわずかに横向きにする（5-15度）
または正面をカメラに向ける
頬杖の手の位置に合わせて自然に傾ける

【四、スタイリングデザイン - 高級ファッションフォーマル】
服装（洗練されたフォーマル＋リラックスしたディテール）：
コアアイテム - 細ストライプのスーツ（参考図2基準）：

✅ ジャケット：

{argument name="suit color" default="ダークカラー"}（黒/ダークグレー/ネイビー）の細ストライプ
スリムフィットまたはスタンダードシルエット
ダブルブレストまたはシングルブレスト
ラペルはくっきり、肩ラインはシャープ

✅ スラックス：

ジャケットと同柄の細ストライプ
ハイウエスト、スリムフィットまたはストレート
裾折り返し（図2重要ディテール参照）

裾を1～2回折り返す
足首と靴下を露出
フォーマルな堅さを和らげ、リラックスしたファッション感を加える

✅ シャツ：

ホワイトフォーマルシャツ
襟元は整え、ボタンは最上まで留めるか微かに緩める
シャツの袖口がスーツの袖口から1-2cmほど見える

靴と靴下：

✅ ブラック光沢レザーシューズ

ダービーシューズまたはオックスフォードシューズ
高度に磨き上げられ、反射が鮮明

✅ 黒のロングソックス（図2の特徴参照）

裾を折り返すため明確に見える
無地または細いストライプ

全体のスタイル：

「高級オーダーメイドスーツ＋リラックスしたファッショナブルなディテール」
「厳格さの中の自由奔放さ」
「洗練されているが堅苦しくない」

アクセサリー（洗練されたディテール）：
1. 細フレーム眼鏡（推奨）：

✅ 金属製細フレーム（ゴールド/シルバー/ブラック）
✅ スクエアまたはラウンドフレーム
✅ 透明レンズ
✅ 「知性的なファッション」の雰囲気をプラス

2. 腕時計：

✅ メタ
```

[[Cinematic Lighting]] [[Identity Locking]] [[Studio Portrait]] [[Editorial Photography]]

### 10. 高定时装冬季主题人像摄影，取景阿尔卑斯山

**Author**: [K](https://x.com/ChillaiKalan__)  **Date**: 2026-01-04  **Language**: en

> 一个高度结构化的提示，旨在生成一张电影感十足、高端时尚的编辑肖像，描绘一位身着奢华冬装的女性，坐落在白雪皑皑的高山环境中一块冰块上。它详细规定了服装、姿势、灯光和相机设置，以实现极致纯净、高端的审美效果。

![高定时装冬季主题人像摄影，取景阿尔卑斯山](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767606990724_ar69da_G91HhyXbgAAWZ-F.jpg)

```
{
  "objective": "Generate a high-fashion winter editorial portrait with a cinematic luxury aesthetic in an alpine environment.",
  "subject": {
    "type": "human",
    "description": "Young woman",
    "pose": {
      "body_position": "Sitting on a sculpted block of ice",
      "legs": "Apart",
      "hand_position": "One gloved hand resting gently against her cheek",
      "expression": "Relaxed yet powerful"
    },
    "wardrobe": {
      "outerwear": "{argument name="outerwear" default="Black oversized puffer jacket"}",
      "pants": "White wide-leg snow pants",
      "footwear": "White luxury winter boots with red laces",
      "accessories": "Plush white fur hat covering ears",

### 11. 动态透视特写转换

**Author**: [Sheetal Shinde](https://x.com/itsSSS1510)  **Date**: 2026-01-04  **Language**: en

> 一个提示，指示 AI 将原始照片转换为四种不同的戏剧性、超逼真、超细节风格。关键特点是使用极端、动态的摄像机角度（低/高网格视图），其中一个身体部位靠近镜头，显得巨大，而身体的其余部分则在透视中强烈后退，同时保持一致的环境和电影般的灯光。

![动态透视特写转换](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767606952014_wcq9ib_G9z-gbKbIAAvyk6.jpg)

Transform the original photo into a dramatic, photorealistic, ultra-detailed set of 4 different styles, each a mid close up wide-angle shot with an extreme, dynamic camera angle (including more grid views from directly below or above), where one or more body parts are positioned right next to the lens and appear huge, the rest of the body recedes strongly in perspective, and the same person strikes a stylish, complex, powerful pose in a consistent, expanded version of the original environment, with cinematic lighting, high contrast, crisp textures, and precise color grading.

> 一个高度受限的提示词，用于生成一张超逼真的高定时装编辑图片，描绘一对情侣在古典艺术博物馆中。它要求姿势与参考图片中的亲密姿态（男士为女士系鞋带）相符，并详细指定了服装（雕塑感白色缎面礼服、剪裁考究的黑色西装）和柔和的电影感博物馆灯光。

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "tool": "NanoBanana Pro",
      "task_type": "photorealistic_couple_high_fashion_editorial",

      "priority": "highest"
    },

    },

      "aspect_ratio": "2:3",
      "orientation": "portrait",
      "resolution": "ultra_high_res",
      "render_style": "ultra_photoreal_high_fashion_editorial",
      "sharpness": "crisp_but_natural",
      "film_grain": "none_or_minimal",
      "color_grade": "soft_museum_cinematic_luxury"
    },
    "hard_constraints": [
      "EXACTLY 2 people only (one woman, one man).",
      "Perfect identity match if reference faces are provided (no face or body changes).",
      "Pose and interaction must match the reference exactly: seated on a museum bench, the man gently fastening the woman’s shoe while she looks at him.",
      "No readable text, no logos, no watermarks.",
      "Perfect anatomy: hands, fingers, legs, feet, and posture fully correct.",
      "Photoreal skin texture; no plastic or over-smoothed skin.",
      "No extra people, reflections, or background faces."
    ],
    "creative_prompt": {
      "scene_summary": "Ultra-photoreal high-fashion editorial set inside a classical art museum gallery. A couple sits on a minimalist stone or wooden bench in front of monumental marble sculptures. The woman wears a sculptural white satin mini dress with exaggerated volume and off-shoulder structure; black high-heel sandals; hair styled in a sleek low bun; minimal refined jewelry. She sits elegantly with one leg slightly extended, looking softly toward the man.\n\nThe man wears an all-black tailored suit with a minimalist shirt, no tie, polished leather shoes. He leans forward, carefully fastening the strap of the woman’s shoe—an intimate, quiet gesture. His posture is focused and gentle, creating a strong emotional narrative.\n\nLighting: soft museum gallery lighting with subtle directional highlights, low contrast, natural shadows, calm cinematic atmosphere. Background: muted green-gray museum walls, large classical marble statues on plinths, discreet signage blurred and unreadable. Color palette: ivory, stone, charcoal, soft sage, warm skin tones. Mood: intimate, elegant, intellectual, timeless, quietly romantic.\n\nCamera: 85mm editorial lens look, medium depth of field; subjects sharply in focus while sculptures fall off gently. Overall feel: luxury fashion house campaign, modern romance, art-meets-couture storytelling."
    },
    "negative_prompt": [
      "any readable text",
      "logos, branding, watermarks",
      "extra people or reflections",
      "distorted legs, hands, or feet",
      "identity drift",
      "cartoon, anime, CGI look",
      "plastic or over-smoothed skin",
      "harsh flash lighting",
      "busy or cluttered"
    ]
  }
}

### 17. 3x3 角色姿势研究网格（萨迪·辛克）

**Author**: [ANKIT PATEL 🇮🇳 | AI](https://x.com/Ankit_patel211)  **Date**: 2026-01-03  **Language**: en

> 一个高度结构化的提示，用于生成同一主体（萨迪·辛克/神奇女侠）的 3x3 超逼真 3D 角色渲染网格。它要求在极简工作室环境中呈现九个独特、复杂的姿势，重点是高角度视角、电影级打光，以及所有九个画面之间绝对的一致性，以打造专业的编辑角色展示。

![3x3 角色姿势研究网格（萨迪·辛克）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767603982069_rx0ri6_G9u9v57bkAEQevH.jpg)

```
Ultra-high quality photorealistic 3D character render presented as a 3x3 image grid (nine frames total), featuring the SAME adult female human subject in nine different poses. Minimalist studio environment with a smooth, seamless light-gray floor and background, no props, no scenery, no text. 

CAMERA & STYLE:
High-angle and slightly top-down perspectives dominate across the grid. Subtle wide-angle lens feel. Photorealistic cinematic 3D render with clean shading, high detail, realistic skin and fabric textures. Professional editorial character showcase. 

POSES GRID ORDER – SAME WOMAN:
1. Squatting slightly with knees bent, arms resting near thighs, looking up at the camera. 
2. Standing upright, relaxed posture, head slightly turned. 
3. Sitting with one knee raised, composed introspective pose. 
4. Standing with hands resting confidently at the waist. 
5. Kneeling and leaning slightly forward, head tilted up, engaged gaze. 
6. Standing with one arm raised gently as if signaling or acknowledging. 
7. Sitting cross-legged, calm and composed posture. 
8. Standing while extending one arm toward the camera in an elegant, interactive gesture. 
9. Lying flat on the back, face looking straight upward, symmetrical composition. 

MOOD & PURPOSE:
Elegant, confident, glamorous, composed. Feels like a professional editorial character turnaround and pose study used for fashion visualization, cinematic previsualization, or high-end portrait rendering. 

RENDER QUALITY:
Ultra-detailed, clean topology, realistic anatomy, smooth gradients, sharp focus, studio-grade output. No noise, no blur, no artifacts. 

CONSISTENCY RULES:
Same face, same body, same hair, same makeup, same outfit, same accessories across all nine frames. No variation drift. 

NEGATIVE PROMPTS:
No background scenery, no environment elements, no text, no logos, no extra characters, no clothing changes, no face variation, no color shifts, no stylization drift, no cartoon or anime look, no distortion, no anatomy errors.
```

### 21. Ultra-photorealistic fashion editorial prompt for urban setting

**Author**: [Lex](https://x.com/lexx_aura)  **Date**: 2026-01-02  **Language**: en

> A detailed, structured prompt designed for ultra-photorealistic fashion editorial images, specifying style, mood, setting, color grading, subject details (female, mid-20s to early 30s, dark hair, matte black outfit), environment, cinematic lighting, and specific camera settings (85mm, f/1.8). It also includes instructions for visual consistency across frames and specific poses, making it ideal for generating a cohesive series of high-end fashion shots.

![Ultra-photorealistic fashion editorial prompt for urban setting](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508434119_y4waqj_G9qQYt0WoAAF91w.jpg)

```
{
  "overall_description": {
    "style": "Ultra-photorealistic fashion editorial",
    "mood": "Moody, cinematic, sensual, confident, urban elegance",
    "setting": "Urban city street with shallow depth of field and blurred traffic lights",
    "time_of_day": "Overcast late afternoon / early evening",
    "color_grading": "Muted earth tones, warm highlights, soft contrast, occasional black-and-white conversion",
    "visual_consistency_rule": "All frames depict the same subject, outfit, hairstyle, environment, pose variations, lighting conditions, and camera characteristics with no deviation"
  },
  "subject": {
    "gender": "Female",
    "age_range": "Mid 20s to early 30s",
    "skin_tone": "Light / fair with warm undertones",
    "face": {
      "features": "Defined cheekbones, full lips, sharp jawline, straight nose",
      "expression": "Calm, confident, slightly intense gaze",
      "makeup": "Natural glam makeup, subtle contour, nude lips, softly defined eyes"
    },
    "hair": {
      "color": "Dark brown",
      "length": "Long",
      "texture": "Voluminous, wavy, slightly tousled",
      "styling": "Loose, windswept, partially covering face in some frames"
    },
    "accessories": {
      "earrings": "Long dangling metallic earrings",
      "other": "No visible necklace or eyewear"
    }
  },
  "outfit": {
    "type": "One-piece jumpsuit or fitted dress",
    "color": "{argument name="outfit color" default="Matte black"}",
    "fit": "Tailored, form-fitting with structured waist",
    "details": {
      "neckline": "Deep V-neck",
      "sleeves": "Long sleeves",
      "belt": "Wide black belt with metal buckle"
    },
    "fabric": "Soft matte fabric with subtle texture"
  },
  "environment": {
    "location": "City street / sidewalk",
    "background_elements": [
      "Out-of-focus buildings",
      "Streetlights and traffic bokeh",
      "Orange traffic cones",
      "Wet or textured pavement"
    ],
    "depth_of_field": "Very shallow, strong background blur",
    "atmosphere": "Urban, slightly gritty yet elegant"
  },
  "lighting": {
    "type": "Natural ambient light",
    "direction": "Soft frontal and side lighting",
    "quality": "Diffused, cinematic",
    "highlights": "Soft highlights on cheekbones and hair",
    "shadows": "Gentle shadows adding facial depth"
  },
  "camera": {
    "camera_type": "Full-frame DSLR or mirrorless",
    "lens": "{argument name="lens" default="85mm prime lens"}",
    "aperture": "{argument name="aperture" default="f/1.8"}",
    "iso": "Low to medium ISO",
    "shutter_speed": "Fast enough to freeze motion",
    "focus": "Sharp focus on subject, background heavily blurred",
    "aspect_ratio": "Vertical portrait (2:3)"
  },
  "poses_and_frames": {
    "frame_1": {

### 36. 带文字牌的圣诞蛋糕提示

**Author**: [田中勇道 | AI愛好家](https://x.com/yudotanaka)  **Date**: 2025-12-22  **Language**: ja

> 为 Nano Banana Pro 生成高质量、垂直海报风格插图的详细提示，内容为一个角色坐在一块奢华的圣诞蛋糕上。提示中明确要求逼真的蛋糕纹理、电影级灯光，以及关键的一点：在蛋糕底部旁边放置一个独立的黑巧克力盘，盘上带有优雅的凸起金色糖霜文字，确保文字清晰可读并完全位于盘内。

![带文字牌的圣诞蛋糕提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766667405926_wxu91z_G8wSb2vawAINE2Y.jpg)
![带文字牌的圣诞蛋糕提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766667406280_m5mci2_G8wSVLObQAA6UNK.jpg)

```
クリーンでプロフェッショナルな構図を持つ、高品質な縦長ポスタースタイルのイラストレーションを作成してください。

**【メインの被写体とアクション】**
参照画像のキャラクターは中央に配置され、豪華にデコレーションされた大きな丸いクリスマスケーキの上端に快適に座っています。

彼女の脚と足は完全に可視化されており、ケーキの側面から少しぶら下がっています。

**【ケーキの描写（※文字の形ではない）**
ケーキ自体は伝統的な円筒形であり、文字によって形成されたものではありません。

リアルな質感を特徴としています

：厚くてふわふわした白いホイップクリームの「雪」、しっとりしたスポンジの層、艶やかな赤いイチゴ、ヒイラギの葉の装飾、そして滴り落ちるイチゴのグレーズ（艶出しシロップ）。

**【テキスト要素と配置】**
ケーキの土台の前面（垂直な面）に、しっかりと取り付けられた「別個の」長方形のダークチョコレートプレートがあります。

このプレートには、盛り上がった金色のアイシングの筆記体で、特定のテキスト「{argument name="好みの文字列" default="好みの文字列（日本語、英語どちらでもOK）"}」が優雅に書かれています。

テキストは完全にプレート内だけに収まっています。

**【環境とライティング】**
背景は、柔らかな金色のボケ光（玉ボケ）、ミニチュアのクリスマス要素、そして舞い落ちる金粉の優しいタッチがある、温かくお祝いムードのあるシーンです。

映画のようなライティング（シネマティックライティング）が、キャラクター、クリーミーなケーキ、そして艶やかなチョコレートプレートの対照的な質感を強調します。

高解像度で、キャラクターとテキストプレートに鋭い焦点が合っています。
```

```
超リアルなデジタルイラストレーション：歴史的な浅草のウォーターフロントから、隅田川越しに見る未来的なスカイツリーの景観。この情景を、四季のサイクルを一つの連続した構図としてシームレスに描く。

左側 (冬)： 冷たい雪景色、雪に覆われた歴史的建造物（外灘の建物）、氷と曇り空の要素。

中央右 (夏)： 豊かな緑の植生、明るい日差し、川面の強い反射、青空と活気に満ちた夏の情景。
右側 (秋)： 黄金色、オレンジ、赤の鮮やかな紅葉の色彩、収穫のムードが漂う晩秋の景色。
季節の間に目に見える境界線は一切なく、天候、照明、植生が滑らかに溶け合い、統一され調和したパノラマを形成する。時の流れを象徴する豊かなディテール、シネマティックな照明、8K解像度、極めて詳細なテクスチャで表現する。

```
Ultra-photorealistic, cinematic macro photography style, capturing an impossible “world inside a cup.”
A white ceramic coffee cup sits on a natural wooden tabletop, filled to the brim with dark coffee. The coffee surface transforms into a turbulent ocean: deep brown waves surge and collide, with realistic coffee crema forming foamy crests, swirling vortices, and complex fluid motion, indistinguishable from a real sea. The rim of the cup is damaged by cannon fire, chipped and broken in several places, implying the intensity of the battle.
Two 18th-century classic pirate sailing ships clash violently inside the cup. The ships are miniature in scale yet extremely detailed: visible wooden hull grain, layered decks, rigging, and weathered sails partially torn and billowing in an unseen sea wind. Portions of the ships rise above the cup’s rim, creating a striking sense of scale contrast and surreal tension.
The scene is frozen at the most dramatic moment of combat. Cannons fire simultaneously from both ships, erupting with bright orange muzzle flashes and thick white smoke that expands within the confined space. The explosions illuminate the ships, sails, and coffee waves, while splashes of liquid burst into the air like seawater caught mid-motion.
Shot from a macro perspective with shallow depth of field, the focus is razor-sharp on the ships and battle action. The background is naturally blurred, revealing only the upper portion of the cup and hints of the surrounding environment. Lighting follows realistic photographic principles, with rich textures and cinematic contrast, creating a highly believable, dramatic, and surreal movie-like moment—tense, epic, and astonishingly lifelike.
--ar 1:1
```

### 87. 奢华夜生活照片拼贴（4 图网格）

**Author**: [Nano banana pro🍌](https://x.com/Vishnudxe)  **Date**: 2026-01-23  **Language**: en

> 一个 JSON 提示模板，用于创建四张（2x2）电影风格的夜生活场景拼贴画，所有画面中人物、服装和地点保持连续性。场景设定为夜晚高档户外餐厅露台，环境光线温暖。人物身着全黑服装（皮夹克、露脐上衣、迷你裙），并展示四种不同的姿势和表情，例如手持酒杯站立或托腮。

![奢华夜生活照片拼贴（4 图网格）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769235972907_g5v1pj_G_Vknf0bAAUeX0J.jpg)

```
{ "scene\_type": "nightlife\_lifestyle", "setting": { "location": "outdoor restaurant or lounge patio", "time": "night", "environment": "urban, intimate, upscale", "lighting": "warm ambient lighting from patio heaters and string lights" }, "composition": { "format": "four-image collage", "layout": "2x2 grid", "continuity": "same subject, outfit, and location across all frames" }, "subject": { "type": "person in the reference image", "appearance": { "hair": { "color": "blonde", "length": "long", "style": "loose, softly waved" } }, "clothing": { "outerwear": "black leather jacket", "top": "black cut-out crop top", "bottom": "black fitted mini skirt" }, "expressions": [ "confident", "relaxed", "contemplative", "posed" ], "poses": [ "standing with wine glass", "seated holding wine glass", "leaning with hands near waist", "resting chin on hand" ] }, "objects": [ { "type": "wine\_glass", "content": "{argument name="drink color" default="red wine"}", "held": true }, { "type": "patio\_heater", "description": "tall outdoor gas heater emitting warm light" }, { "type": "met" 

First, define the scene as a nighttime outdoor restaurant or lounge patio. The environment should feel urban, intimate, and premium. Use warm ambient lighting such as patio heaters and string lights to create a cozy yet luxurious night atmosphere.

Next, make sure visual continuity is locked. Use the same subject, outfit, and location in all images. This consistency is what gives the final collage a professional, editorial feel.

Style the subject in a full black nightlife outfit. A black leather jacket paired with a black cut-out crop top and a fitted black mini skirt works perfectly for a confident and modern look. The hair should be long, blonde, loose, and softly waved to maintain an effortless nightlife vibe.

Across the four frames, vary the subject’s expressions and poses. One image can show the subject standing confidently while holding a glass of red wine. Another can be seated and relaxed with the wine glass in hand. A third pose can involve leaning slightly with hands near the waist for a composed look. The final frame can be more contemplative, with the subject resting their chin on their hand.

When generated correctly, Nano Banana Pro will produce a high-end nightlife photo collage that feels cinematic, stylish, and social-media ready, suitable for fashion editorials, lifestyle branding, and premium AI visuals. Share your nightlife photo collages below!
```

```
A cinematic wide rooftop shot of a beautiful woman seated at the edge of a weathered concrete ledge, viewed from behind and centered in frame, overlooking a vast city engulfed in distant fires and explosions, with burning skyscrapers glowing through thick smoke; shot on a Panavision Millennium DXL2

with a Panavision C-Series 35mm lens at aperture 1/4, creating an extremely shallow depth of field that melts the city lights into warm, abstract bokeh while keeping her silhouette and the rooftop edge subtly defined; the camera sits at seated eye level behind her with a slight downward angle, emphasizing scale, isolation, and quiet strength: lighting comes primarily from diffused orange and amber firelight wrapping the scene in haze, contrasted by a faint cool blue-gray rim light separating her figure; the color palette blends burnt orange, copper highlights, deep charcoal shadows, and desaturated blues with soft contrast, lifted blacks, gentle bloom, and fine film grain; the mood is somber, poetic, and contemplative; visible elements include cracked damp concrete reflecting firelight, drifting smoke and embers, glowing windows, and faint traffic trails below; a beautiful moment of stillness against an apocalyptic cityscape.

### 112. 冰下超现实概念肖像 (JSON 格式)

**Author**: [Oogie](https://x.com/oggii_0)  **Date**: 2025-12-18  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张电影般、超现实且情绪化的概念摄影作品，描绘一位年轻女性被冰冻表面淹没的场景。该提示详细说明了拍摄对象的姿势（向上看，手按在冰面上）、透过冰层过滤的冷色调光线，以及碎冰、霜和被困气泡的纹理细节，以营造出一种令人难以忘怀的美丽而孤寂的氛围。

![冰下超现实概念肖像 (JSON 格式)](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766237914016_mpdwbc_G8c_KlxbEAAAcst.jpg)

```
{
  "subject": {
    "description": "Young woman submerged beneath a frozen surface",
    "pose": "Looking upward through the ice, right hand pressed flat against the underside of the surface",
    "expression": "Calm, slightly melancholic, direct gaze",
    "visible_parts": "Face and right hand clearly visible, body obscured by ice texture"
  },
  "face": {
    "skin_tone": "Pale, porcelain-like",
    "eyes": "Blue-grey, sharp focus, looking directly at viewer",

The eyes become more inhuman and menacing, glowing faintly with a cursed inner intensity while still matching the original face placement. His hair begins to grow out in a wild, uneven, primitive way during the transformation - thin at first, then spreading into rough, dark, feral strands, as if his body is rapidly reverting into some ancient night-creature form. Small stray strands emerge around the scalp, temples, and crown, becoming messy, coarse, and aggressive. The beard and stubble also thicken slightly in a raw, untamed way. The final form is not a completely different creature, but a horrifying evolved version of the same man - an ancient vampire warrior, primal, savage, and intelligent. He leans slightly toward the camera like a predator about to strike. His breathing is heavier now, teeth fully visible, fangs wet, facial muscles trembling with contained violence. ### 153. 超电影感红色剪影肖像，带双重曝光

**Author**: [Professor](https://x.com/Professor_134)  **Date**: 2026-03-13  **Language**: en

> 一个针对 Google Nano Banana 2 的高度具体的提示，要求生成一张超电影感、戏剧性的红色剪影肖像，描绘一位年轻男子的侧面轮廓，其面部和发型需与上传的图片 100% 一致。该提示强调高对比度的红色照明、发光的轮廓光、象征内心冲突的双重曝光阴影效果，以及超现实的细节。

![超电影感红色剪影肖像，带双重曝光](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773469807705_3yr78p_HDQwo_4bQAACZKk.jpg)

```
Generate an Ultra-cinematic dramatic red silhouette portrait of a young man in side profile, captured from the shoulders up, standing in a contemplative pose. The man has messy textured hair and a short rugged beard, ( keep face and hair style 100% same as in uploaded image) wearing a casual dark hoodie with soft fabric folds and realistic cloth texture. His eyes are closed and his fingers gently touch his temple, suggesting deep thought, emotional tension, or inner conflict.

The lighting is extremely dramatic monochromatic red cinematic lighting, creating a powerful high-contrast visual style. A bright red backlight outlines the man’s silhouette, producing glowing rim light along his hair, face profile, beard, and hoodie edges. The front of the figure remains mostly in shadow, creating a deep black silhouette with subtle red highlights.

Behind him appears a large ghostly double-exposure shadow of the same person, facing the opposite direction. This secondary silhouette is slightly blurred and darker, creating a psychological duality effect, symbolizing inner thoughts or conflict. The layered composition creates depth and visual storytelling.

The background is minimalistic and atmospheric, consisting of a smooth red-to-dark gradient with soft volumetric haze and drifting smoke particles surrounding the figure. The smoke catches the red lighting, creating glowing mist around the silhouette.

Hair strands, beard texture, hoodie fabric fibers, and skin contours are subtly visible through the dramatic lighting, adding hyper-realistic detail. The lighting creates strong chiaroscuro contrast, emphasizing the emotional and cinematic mood.

Composition follows professional cinematic portrait framing, with strong negative space and balanced silhouette placement. The scene feels like a movie poster or psychological thriller artwork.

### 199. 昏暗餐厅中的高对比度闪光人像提示词

**Author**: [Sadia](https://x.com/SadiaMalik182)  **Date**: 2026-01-21  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一张年轻女性在高对比度肖像，她坐在一间光线昏暗的豪华餐厅里。提示中指定了她的姿势（双手抱头）、着装（白色露背迷你连衣裙），并要求使用强烈的机顶闪光灯照明来营造深邃的阴影。

![昏暗餐厅中的高对比度闪光人像提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063229058_7lee42_G_L_o3CbQAA9R7q.jpg)

```
•.° - ₊˚ʚ ɞ˚₊ - °.•

Create an image of a young woman. Do not change my face

Pose/Expression:
- She is sitting on a deep red leather banquette that curves around the table. She is leaning forward slightly toward the camera. 
- Both elbows are resting on the table. Her hands are brought up to her head, with her palms gently cradling her temples and her fingers tucked into her hair, creating a soft, contemplative frame for her face. Looking directly to camera lens with a neutral, soft expression.
- Her hips face to the right, with her upper body slightly turned back toward the camera. Crossed-legs at the edge of the table, creating a compact pose. Her lower legs and feet are partly out of frame, but appear tucked back or angled toward the floor.

Outfit/Accessories:
- She is wearing a white halter-neck mini dress. The dress has a high mock-neck collar with a small keyhole cutout at the chest. It features a sleeveless, open-back high-neck design that highlights the shoulders. Made from lightweight, slightly sheer chiffon or organza, it has a bubble or tiered hem that creates a soft, airy shape against the fitted neckline.
- A classic gold-tone wristwatch with a metallic link bracelet, worn on the left wrist.
- Soft beige coffin shape glossy nails

Hair:
- Chest-length black-colored hair with subtle waves. Styled with curtain bangs that framing her face

Makeup:
- She wears soft glam makeup with a natural, luminous finish. Neutral champagne eyeshadow with a subtle shimmer, softly blended brown crease, and thin eyeliner. Long, wispy lashes. Lightly defined brows. Soft peach or rose blush. Nude-pink glossy lips. Elegant, effortless night-time beauty suitable for a dim-lit restaurant setting.

Setting/Background:
- A dimly lit restaurant setting, captured with a blend of elegant and candid aesthetics.
- Behind her is a plain but luxurious looking white wall (on right) and on left side is an ornate display cabinet with glass doors and internal lighting. It houses various glassware (wine and water glasses)
- A dark wood circular table is visible, set with a dark ceramic plate, polished silver cutlery, and a folded patterned table napkin.

Lighting:
- There is a soft glow from direct camera flash hitting her face and shoulder.
- The subject is illuminated by a strong direct on-camera flash. Creating strong contrast and deep shadows in the background. No ambient light, naturally dim atmosphere.

Angle & Framing:
- The shot is taken from a slightly high angle, looking down at the subject.
- It is a medium-full shot. The frame captures her from the head down to her mid-thigh, including a significant portion of the table
```

### 200. 电影级黄金时段人像提示词

**Author**: [Harboriis](https://x.com/harboriis)  **Date**: 2026-01-20  **Language**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于生成一张电影般的、内省的年轻男子肖像。他身着正装（马甲），坐在一间高档复古餐厅里，利用“黄金时段”的阳光从侧面投射出戏剧性的光线，在墙上投下清晰的剪影。

![电影级黄金时段人像提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768977319267_giiw13_G_G-nzyWQAAqEqk.jpg)

```
Core Subject & Pose
Subject: A young man with thick, dark curly hair captured in a sharp side profile.
Pose: Seated in a relaxed but grounded posture on a dark {argument name="seat color" default="green"} ribbed leather booth. One arm is draped casually along the top of the backrest, and the head is turned away, looking toward a light source.

Attire & Accessories
Clothing: A dark charcoal-grey formal waistcoat (vest) worn over a crisp white button-down shirt. The shirt is unbuttoned at the collar and the sleeves are rolled up to the mid-forearm.
Detailing: Subtle accessories including a silver link watch on the left wrist, a minimalist silver bracelet, and a statement ring on the right hand.

Environment & Background
Setting:An upscale, vintage-style restaurant or cafe interior.
Wall Details: A clean white paneled/wainscoted wall featuring a small, minimalist framed black-and-white architectural sketch and an antique brass wall sconce with a spherical glass bulb.
Foreground: A corner of a light wood table with a white cloth napkin and silver cutlery.

Lighting & Atmosphere
Light Source: Strong, low-angle "golden hour" sunlight streaming in from the side.
Visual Effects: Dramatic side-lighting that creates a sharp, recognizable silhouette shadow of the subject’s profile onto the white wall behind him.
Mood: Introspective, cinematic, and sophisticated, with high contrast between the warm sunbeams and the deep green of the leather.
```
